‚Äì –†–∞–∑—É–º–µ–µ—Ç—Å—è. –ù–µ—Ç –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫–∏—Ö –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω —á—Ç–æ-–ª–∏–±–æ –ø–æ–¥–æ–∑—Ä–µ–≤–∞–µ—Ç. –ò –ú–∞–π–∫–ª —Ç–æ–∂–µ.
‚Äì –í—Å–µ –¥–∞—Ç—ã —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—é—Ç‚Ä¶ –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç, –¢–µ–º–µ—à–≤–∞—Ä –∑–∞–±–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–µ–ª–∞ –≤–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–∏—è. –û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –≤ –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ–º –¥–µ–ª–µ –Ω–µ—Ç –Ω–∏ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞ –æ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω–∞ –≤–µ—Ä–Ω—É–ª–∞—Å—å –Ω–∞ –±–∞–∑—É –±–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π ‚Äì –≤–ø—Ä–æ—á–µ–º, –∏ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ—Ç –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –∏ –æ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –±–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —è–≤–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–æ–π –µ–µ –≤—ã—Ö–æ–¥–∞ –≤ –æ—Ç—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∫—É —Å–ø—É—Å—Ç—è –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–µ–≤. –ó–¥–µ—Å—å —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–æ–¥—è—Ç—Å—è —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞ —Å–∞–º–æ–π –¢–µ–º–µ—à–≤–∞—Ä, —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–≤—à–µ–π, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω–∞, —Ü–∏—Ç–∏—Ä—É—é: ¬´‚Ä¶–ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è–ª–∞ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å –∫ —Å–ª—É–∂–µ–±–Ω–æ–π –∫–∞—Ä—å–µ—Ä–µ¬ª. –ß—Ç–æ –∂, –º–æ–≥—É –µ–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è—Ç—å. –®–µ—Å—Ç—å –º–µ—Å—è—Ü–µ–≤ –Ω–∞–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ —Å –ú–∞—Ä–∫—É—Å–æ–º ‚Äì –Ω–∏–∫—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –≤—ã–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç.
‚Äì –ü—Ä–æ—à—É –≤–∞—Å –æ—Ç–º–µ—Ç–∏—Ç—å, ‚Äì —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª –õ–æ–º–±–æ–∫, ‚Äì —á—Ç–æ –ê–ª—å–ø–∏–Ω –±—ã–ª –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–º –ø—É–Ω–∫—Ç–æ–º –∏—Ö –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∏ –Ω–∞ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ–º –ø—É—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –±–∞–∑—É ¬´–ö–û–†–°–ï–ö¬ª. –ü–æ—Ö–æ–∂–µ, –¢–µ–º–µ—à–≤–∞—Ä –±–ª–∞–≥–æ–ø–æ–ª—É—á–Ω–æ –∏–∑–±–∞–≤–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –æ—Ç –±–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–æ–π –∂–µ –Ω–∞—Å–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–µ –∏ –Ω–∏ —Å–ª–æ–≤–æ–º –Ω–µ –æ–±–º–æ–ª–≤–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –æ–± —ç—Ç–æ–º –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –≤—Ä–∞—á–∞–º.
‚Äì –î–∞‚Ä¶ –¥–∞‚Ä¶ –Ø –Ω–∞ –¥–æ—Å—É–≥–µ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–µ–Ω—å–∫–æ –æ–±–¥—É–º–∞—é –≤—Å–µ —ç—Ç–æ. –ê –ø–æ–∫–∞ –Ω–∞–º –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–∂–Ω–æ.
‚Äì –ê–Ω–∂–µ–ª–æ, —É —Ç–µ–±—è –Ω–∞ –ª–∏—Ü–µ –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ —Ç—ã —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –∑–∞–º—ã—Å–ª–∏–ª –∏ –∂–¥–µ—à—å –º–æ–µ–≥–æ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è.
‚Äì –ü–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞—é, –º–Ω–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ —É–∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–æ—Å—å —Å –≠–ª–ª–∏ –¢–µ–º–µ—à–≤–∞—Ä. –í—Å—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç–∏—Ç—å—Å—è —Å –Ω–µ–π. –ü–æ–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—Å—è, –¥–∞–∂–µ –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –µ–µ –ø–æ–¥ –∫–∞–∫–∏–º-–ª–∏–±–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–≥–æ–º –Ω–∞ –õ—É–Ω–Ω—É—é –ë–∞–∑—É.
‚Äì –≠—Ç–æ –ø–æ–º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ª—É—á—à–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è—Ç—å –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞, –ø—Ä–µ–¥—É–≥–∞–¥–∞—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–∏–º –æ–Ω —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–µ—Ç. –ê –∏–∑ –µ–µ –ª–∏—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞, –ø–æ-–º–æ–µ–º—É, –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ —É–∑–Ω–∞–µ—à—å.
‚Äì –ï–µ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â–µ–µ –º–µ—Å—Ç–æ–∂–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∏–∑–≤–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ?
‚Äì –û–Ω–∞ –∂–∏–≤–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ –ó–µ–º–ª–µ. –ü–æ –∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ–π –º–µ—Ä–µ, –∂–∏–ª–∞ —Ç–∞–º –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—à–ª–æ–º –≥–æ–¥—É. –¢–æ–≥–¥–∞ –æ–Ω–∞ —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è—Ç—å —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–∏–µ –≤ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ–π –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ø–∏—Å–∏ –Ω–∞—Å–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è. –ñ–∏–≤–µ—Ç –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ –≤ –•—Ä–∞–º–µ –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≥–æ –°–ø–∞—Å–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è.
‚Äì –ü–æ—Ö–æ–∂–µ, —ç—Ç–æ —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ —Å —Ä–µ–ª–∏–≥–∏–µ–π. –ü—Ä–∞–≤–¥–∞, —è –æ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –Ω–µ —Å–ª—ã—à–∞–ª.
‚Äì –ò —è —Ç–æ–∂–µ. –í–ø—Ä–æ—á–µ–º, –æ–Ω–∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ –≤–æ–∑–Ω–∏–∫–∞—é—Ç –∏ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–∞—é—Ç.
–¢—É–ø–µ–ª–æ–≤ –ø–æ–º–æ–ª—á–∞–ª. –ó–∞—Å—É–Ω—É–≤ –ø–∞–ª–µ—Ü –≤ —Ä–æ—Ç, –æ–Ω –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—è–ª—Å—è –æ–±–≥—Ä—ã–∑–∞—Ç—å –∑–∞—É—Å–µ–Ω–µ—Ü.
‚Äì –°–æ–º–Ω–µ–≤–∞—é—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑—É–º–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–æ–∑–∏—Ç—å —Å—é–¥–∞ –¢–µ–º–µ—à–≤–∞—Ä –ø—Ä—è–º–æ —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å. –≠—Ç–æ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–ª–µ—á–µ—Ç –∏–∑–ª–∏—à–Ω–µ–µ –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ.
‚Äì –ò –≤—Å–µ –∂–µ —è –ø—Ä–æ—à—É –≤–∞—à–µ–π —Å–∞–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏. –Ø –±—É–¥—É –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ –æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–∂–Ω–æ. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —Å—Ç–æ–ª–∫–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –ì–æ—Ä–ª–æ–≤–∏–Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–∏—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –≤—Ä–∞–≥ –¥–æ–≥–∞–¥—ã–≤–∞–ª—Å—è –æ —á—Ä–µ–∑–≤—ã—á–∞–π–Ω–æ–π –≤–∞–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞—à–µ–π –º–∏—Å—Å–∏–∏. –°–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, —Ç–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å –µ–º—É —Å–∫–æ—Ä–µ–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ –∏–∑–≤–µ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –∑–¥–µ—Å—å. –í —Å–∞–º–æ–µ –±–ª–∏–∂–∞–π—à–µ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –±–µ—Ä—Å–µ—Ä–∫–µ—Ä—ã —Å–æ–æ–±—â–∞—Ç –æ–± —ç—Ç–æ–º —Å–≤–æ–∏–º –ø—Ä–∏—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–∏–∫–∞–º –Ω–∞ –ó–µ–º–ª–µ, –¥–æ–±—Ä–æ–∂–∏–ª–∞–º. –ù–µ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –∏—Å–∫–ª—é—á–∞—Ç—å –≤–µ—Ä–æ—è—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ç–æ–∂–µ –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è—Ç, –∫—Ç–æ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ä–æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä—å—é –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫–∞. –î–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞ —É—Å—ã–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –Ω–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω—ã–º–∏, –Ω–æ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–¥–æ –∑–∞–±—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –æ–Ω –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –ê–ª—å–ø–∏–Ω–µ.
‚Äì –î–∞-–¥–∞, –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–π –ø—Ä–æ–∫–ª—è—Ç–æ–π –ø–ª–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–µ‚Ä¶ –•–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ, –ê–Ω–∂–µ–ª–æ, –µ—Å–ª–∏ —Ç—ã —Ç–∞–∫ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—à—å‚Ä¶
–ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–∫–∏–¥–∞–ª–æ –æ—â—É—â–µ–Ω–∏–µ, —á—Ç–æ —Å–æ–±—ã—Ç–∏—è —Å–ª–∏—à–∫–æ–º —Ç–æ—Ä–æ–ø—è—Ç.
–û–Ω –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –õ—É–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ë–∞–∑–µ —á—É—Ç—å –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ –¥–Ω—è, –∞ –µ–≥–æ —É–∂–µ –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π —Ä–∞–∑ –æ–¥–µ–≤–∞—é—Ç –≤ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª. –ö —Ç–æ–º—É –∂–µ —Ç–µ–ø–µ—Ä—å —ç—Ç–æ –µ–≥–æ –µ–¥–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–∞. –ü–ª–∞—Ç—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ –≥—Ä—É–∑–æ–≤–æ–≥–æ –ª–∏—Ñ—Ç–∞ –ø–æ–¥–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫ –ª–∏—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –≤–æ–∑–¥—É—Ö–∞ –∑–∞–º–æ—Ä–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –Ω–æ—á–Ω—ã–º —Ö–æ–ª–æ–¥–æ–º –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ö–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏, –∏ —Å—Ç–æ —Å –ª–∏—à–Ω–∏–º –≤–∑—Ä–æ—Å–ª—ã—Ö, –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥—è—â–∏—Ö—Å—è –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ–π, ‚Äì –≤–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, —É—á–µ–Ω—ã—Ö, —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤, ‚Äì –≤—Å–µ –¥–æ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–¥–µ—Ç—ã –≤ —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä—ã‚Ä¶ –ù—É, –ø–æ—á—Ç–∏ –≤—Å–µ. –§—Ä—ç–Ω–∫, –ø–æ –µ–≥–æ —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞–º, —Å–æ —Å–≤–æ–∏–º —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä–æ–º –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ —Ä–∞—Å—Å—Ç–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è.
–ï–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä—ã —É—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏–ª–∏—Å—å —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∞ –æ—Ç –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞, –∞ —Å–ª–µ–≤–∞ —Å—Ç–æ—è–ª –Ω–∞—É—á–Ω—ã–π —Ä—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∞ –¥–æ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –≠–¥–º–æ–Ω–¥ –ô–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏. –ï–≥–æ –Ω–µ–∫—Ä–∞—Å–∏–≤—ã–µ —Ä–∞—Å–∫–æ—Å—ã–µ –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞ –Ω–µ –æ—Ç—Ä—ã–≤–∞—è—Å—å —Å–ª–µ–¥–∏–ª–∏ –∑–∞ –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫–æ–º —Å–∫–≤–æ–∑—å —Å—Ç–µ–∫–ª–æ –≥–µ—Ä–º–æ—à–ª–µ–º–∞.
‚Äì –í—Å–µ –≤ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–∫–µ? ‚Äì —Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª –¥–æ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –ô–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏.
‚Äì –Ø –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —Ö–æ—Ç–µ–ª –µ—â–µ —Ä–∞–∑ —É–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å—Å—è.
–®–ª—é–∑–æ–≤–∞—è –∫–∞–º–µ—Ä–∞ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–ª–∞—Å—å, –∏ –≤–æ–∑–¥—É—Ö –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª –≤—ã—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞—Ä—É–∂—É. –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—É–ø—Ä–µ–¥–∏–ª–∏, —á—Ç–æ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏—Ç –µ–≥–æ –≤—Å–µ–º –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–º –¥–ª—è –¥—ã—Ö–∞–Ω–∏—è –≤–æ–∑–¥—É—Ö–æ–º ‚Äì —Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ–µ, –∫–∏—Å–ª–æ—Ä–æ–¥–æ–º. –ù–µ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä—è –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ —á—Ç–æ –¥–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–∞—é—â–µ–≥–æ –≥–∞–∑–∞ –ø–∞–¥–∞–ª–æ, –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–ª —Å–µ–±—è —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –∫–æ–º—Ñ–æ—Ä—Ç–Ω–æ –≤ –ª—è–º–∫–∞—Ö –Ω–µ–æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä–∞, –ø–æ—Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—ã–≤–∞—é—â–∏—Ö —Å–ª–æ–≤–Ω–æ –∂–µ—Å—Ç–∫–∏–µ –±—É–º–∞–∂–Ω—ã–µ –∫—Ä—ã–ª—å—è. –°–∏–ª–æ–≤—ã–µ –ø–æ–ª—è —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ –ø–æ—á—Ç–∏ –Ω–µ–æ—Å—è–∑–∞–µ–º—ã–º–∏ –∏ –Ω–µ–≤–∏–¥–∏–º—ã–º–∏, –∏ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –Ω–µ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–ª —Å–µ–±—è —Å—Ç–µ—Å–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º.
–ù–∞–±–ª—é–¥–∞–≤—à–∏–π –∑–∞ –Ω–∏–º –≤—Ä–∞—á –Ω–µ–±—Ä–µ–∂–Ω–æ –∑–∞–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª:
‚Äì –ê —Ç—ã –≤—Å–µ –µ—â–µ –¥—ã—à–∏—à—å.
–≠—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–æ —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å—Ä–µ–¥–Ω–µ–µ –º–µ–∂–¥—É –≤–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å–æ–º –∏ —É—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º.
‚Äì –î–∞, ‚Äì —Å–º—É—â–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–¥–∏–ª –ú–∞–π–∫–ª.
–í –µ–≥–æ –¥—ã—Ö–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—É—Ç—è—Ö –ø–æ-–ø—Ä–µ–∂–Ω–µ–º—É –æ—â—É—â–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –¥–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤–æ–∑–¥—É—Ö–∞ ‚Äì —Ç–æ—á–Ω–µ–µ, –Ω–µ—á—Ç–æ –∑–∞–º–µ–Ω—è—é—â–µ–µ –¥–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤–æ–∑–¥—É—Ö–∞; –Ω–µ—Å–æ–º–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω–æ, —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –∑–∞–∫—É–ø–æ—Ä–∏–≤–∞–ª–æ –µ–≥–æ –Ω–æ—Å –∏ —Ä–æ—Ç, –Ω–µ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—è —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–º—É –ª–µ–≥–∫–∏—Ö –≤—ã—Ä–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞—Ä—É–∂—É. –û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ–º —ç–∫—Å–ø–µ—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª—É –≤–∫—Ä–∞—Ç—Ü–µ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏–ª–∏ ‚Äì –ø—Ä–∞–≤–¥–∞, –æ–Ω –∏–∑ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ—á—Ç–∏ –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–Ω—è–ª, ‚Äì –∫–∞–∫ —Å–∏–ª–æ–≤—ã–µ –ø–æ–ª—è ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç–∞¬ª, –≤ —Ç—ã—Å—è—á–∞—Ö —Ç–æ—á–µ–∫ –±–µ–∑–±–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –ø—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∫–∞—è —Å–∫–≤–æ–∑—å –∫–æ–∂—É, —Å–Ω–∞–±–∂–∞—é—Ç —Ç–µ–ª–æ –≤—Å–µ–º –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–º –∏ –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥—è—Ç –æ—Ç—Ö–æ–¥—ã –∂–∏–∑–Ω–µ–¥–µ—è—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏. –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –æ–±–Ω–∞—Ä—É–∂–∏–ª, —á—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –∑–∞—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å–µ–±—è –ø—Ä–µ–∫—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—å –¥—ã—à–∞—Ç—å, –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —á–µ–≥–æ –≤—Å–µ –¥—ã—Ö–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ—Ñ–ª–µ–∫—Å—ã –æ–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –ø–æ–¥–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏.
–ï—â–µ –º–≥–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏–µ ‚Äì –∏ –æ–Ω –∑–∞–±—ã–ª, —á—Ç–æ —É –Ω–µ–≥–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å —Ç–µ–ª–æ. –ú–∞—Å—Å–∏–≤–Ω—ã–µ –¥–≤–µ—Ä—Ü—ã –Ω–∞–¥ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–π —Ä–∞–∑–¥–≤–∏–Ω—É–ª–∏—Å—å, –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–µ–±–æ.
–ñ–∏—Ç–µ–ª–∏ –ê–ª—å–ø–∏–Ω–∞ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –æ—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –≤–∏–¥—è—Ç –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥—ã. –ü–æ—Ä–æ–π –≤ —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–π —Ç—É–º–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–Ω–µ–π, –∞ —Ç–æ –∏ –Ω–µ–¥–µ–ª—å –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è ¬´–æ–∫–Ω–æ¬ª, –∏ –∫—Ä–æ—à–µ—á–Ω—ã–π –ø—è—Ç–∞—á–æ–∫ –Ω–µ–±–æ—Å–≤–æ–¥–∞ –Ω–∞–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å–≤–µ—Ç–æ–º –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥. –í —Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö —Å–ª—É—á–∞—è—Ö –ª—é–¥–∏ –Ω–æ—á–∞–º–∏ –≤—ã—Å—ã–ø–∞—é—Ç –Ω–∞ —É–ª–∏—Ü—É –∏ —á–∞—Å–∞–º–∏ —Å—Ç–æ—è—Ç, –∑–∞–¥—Ä–∞–≤ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤—ã –≤–≤–µ—Ä—Ö.
–ó–∞ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –ø—É—Ç–µ—à–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è —Å –ê–ª—å–ø–∏–Ω–∞ –Ω–∞ –õ—É–Ω–Ω—É—é –ë–∞–∑—É, –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–µ–∫–∞–≤—à–µ–≥–æ, –µ—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å —Å—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –ì–æ—Ä–ª–æ–≤–∏–Ω–µ, —Å–ø–æ–∫–æ–π–Ω–æ, –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –≤–ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ –≤ –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏–ª –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–µ–Ω—å–∫–æ —Ä–∞—Å—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ —Å—Ç–∞—Ä–∏–Ω–∫–µ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –ú–ª–µ—á–Ω—ã–º –ü—É—Ç–µ–º. –ù–æ –æ–¥–Ω–æ –¥–µ–ª–æ ‚Äì —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥—ã —Å–∫–≤–æ–∑—å —Å—Ç–µ–∫–ª–æ –∏–ª–ª—é–º–∏–Ω–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞. –°–µ–π—á–∞—Å –∂–µ –Ω–µ–±–æ –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º. –õ–∏—Ñ—Ç, –ø–æ–¥–Ω—è–≤—à–∏—Å—å –≤—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å —Å –ª—É–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ö–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é, –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏–ª—Å—è. –ó–µ–º–ª—è –∏ –°–æ–ª–Ω—Ü–µ –ø—Ä—è—Ç–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –∑–∞ –≥–æ—Ä–∏–∑–æ–Ω—Ç–æ–º, –∏ –≤—Å–µ –±–µ—Å–∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–∞–¥ –≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–π –±—ã–ª–æ —É—Å—ã–ø–∞–Ω–æ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥–∞–º–∏.
–≠—Ç–æ –≤–µ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –∑—Ä–µ–ª–∏—â–µ –Ω–µ –≤—Å–µ–ª–∏–ª–æ –≤ –¥—É—à—É –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫–∞ —É–∂–∞—Å–∞ –ª–∏—à—å –ø–æ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–µ: –¥–æ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥ –±—ã–ª–æ –±–µ—Å–∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ –¥–∞–ª–µ–∫–æ.
–ü—Ä–∏—â—É—Ä–∏–≤—à–∏—Å—å, –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –ø–æ–¥–Ω—è–ª –ø—Ä–∞–≤—É—é —Ä—É–∫—É. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥ —Ç–µ–º –∫–∞–∫ –∑–∞–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å, –æ–Ω –ø–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤—ã—á–∫–µ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–ª –≤–¥–æ—Ö, –∏ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–∑–≤—É—á–∞–ª–∏ –æ—Ç—á–µ—Ç–ª–∏–≤–æ, –∞ —Ä–∞–¥–∏–æ–ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç—á–∏–∫ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç–∞¬ª –¥–æ–Ω–µ—Å –∏—Ö –¥–æ –Ω–∞—É—à–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤ –≤ —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä–∞—Ö –Ω–∞–±–ª—é–¥–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π.
‚Äì –¢—ã –∏–º–µ–µ—à—å –≤ –≤–∏–¥—É —ç—Ç–∏ —Ç—Ä–∏ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥—ã, —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–∞ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π –ª–∏–Ω–∏–∏? ‚Äì –Ω–µ—É–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç–∏–ª –ô–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏. ‚Äì –≠—Ç–æ –û—Ä–∏–æ–Ω, –ü–æ—è—Å –û—Ö–æ—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–∞. –¢–µ–±–µ –∑–Ω–∞–∫–æ–º—ã –Ω–∞—à–∏ —Å–æ–∑–≤–µ–∑–¥–∏—è?
‚Äì –ù–µ—Ç, –Ω–µ —ç—Ç–∏ —Ç—Ä–∏ –∑–≤–µ–∑–¥—ã. ‚Äì –ú–∞–π–∫–ª —Ç–∫–Ω—É–ª –≤ –Ω–µ–±–æ –ø–∞–ª—å—Ü–µ–º, –∏ –≤—Å–ª–µ–¥ –∑–∞ –µ–≥–æ —Ä—É–∫–æ–π –ø–∞—Ä–∞–±–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ –≤–∏—Ö—Ä—è–º–∏ –≤–∑–º–µ—Ç–Ω—É–ª–∏—Å—å —Å–µ—Ä–µ–±—Ä–∏—Å—Ç—ã–µ –≤–æ–ª–Ω—ã. ‚Äì
–û–Ω –≤–∏–¥–µ–ª —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ –æ—Å–ª–µ–ø–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —è—Ä–∫–æ–µ, —Ä–∞—Å–∫—Ä–∞—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –≤ —Ç–∞–∫–∏–µ —Ü–≤–µ—Ç–∞, –ø–æ–¥–æ–±–Ω—ã—Ö –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–º –æ–Ω –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–µ–ª. –ú–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫ –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥ –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–ª–æ–≤, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —É–≤–∏–¥–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ.
‚Äì –¢–µ–ª–µ—Ü?..
–ò –≤–¥—Ä—É–≥ –¥–æ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ –¥–æ—à–ª–æ, —á—Ç–æ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä—è—Ç –Ω–µ–≤–æ–æ—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –≤–∑–≥–ª—è–¥–æ–º –∏ –Ω–µ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç –æ–Ω. –û—Å–ª–µ–ø–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ —Å–∏—è–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –≤ —É–ª—å—Ç—Ä–∞–∫–æ—Ä–æ—Ç–∫–æ–≤–æ–ª–Ω–æ–≤–æ–π —Ä–∞–¥–∏–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–π —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ —ç–ª–µ–∫—Ç—Ä–æ–º–∞–≥–Ω–∏—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–ø–µ–∫—Ç—Ä–∞, –∏ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–ª –≥–ª–∞–∑—É –≤–∏–¥–µ—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ.
–ù–∞—á–∞–ª–∏—Å—å –ø—Ä–∏–≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–º –∏—Å–ø—ã—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è–º –≤ –±–µ–∑–≤–æ–∑–¥—É—à–Ω–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ. –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –æ—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –ø–æ–¥–Ω–∏–º–∞–ª –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞ –∫ –Ω–µ–±—É. –ü–æ—Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–Ω –Ω–∞—É—á–∏–ª—Å—è —É–º–µ–Ω—å—à–∞—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–Ω—Å–∏–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–≤–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ç–∞–∫, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –æ–Ω–æ –µ–≥–æ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ –Ω–µ —Å–ª–µ–ø–∏–ª–æ, –∏ –≤ —Ç–æ –∂–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã —É–≤–µ–ª–∏—á–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫. –û–±–ª–∞–∫–æ –≥–∞–∑–∞ —Å —Ä–≤–∞–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∫—Ä–∞—è–º–∏ ‚Äì –≥–∏–≥–∞–Ω—Ç—Å–∫–∏–π –≤–∑—Ä—ã–≤, –∑–∞—Å—Ç—ã–≤—à–∏–π –≤–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏. –ö–∞–∫ –¥–æ –Ω–µ–≥–æ –¥–∞–ª–µ–∫–æ? –ù–∞–≤–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–µ, –Ω–µ –º–µ–Ω—å—à–µ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏—Ö —Å–æ—Ç–µ–Ω —Å–≤–µ—Ç–æ–≤—ã—Ö –ª–µ—Ç.
–®–∞—Ö—Ç–∞ –ª–∏—Ñ—Ç–∞ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–∞—Å—å –≤ —Å–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∏–Ω–µ —Ä–æ–≤–Ω–æ–π –ø–ª–æ—â–∞–¥–∫–∏ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–ª–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–∞–∑–∞–ª—å—Ç–∞ –ø–ª–æ—â–∞–¥—å—é –≤ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≥–µ–∫—Ç–∞—Ä–æ–≤, –∞ —Å–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω –µ–µ –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–∞–ª–∏ –∑–∞—Å—Ç—ã–≤—à–∏–µ –≤–æ–ª–Ω—ã —Ä–µ–≥–æ–ª–∏—Ç–∞, –∫–∏–ª–æ–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö –≤ –¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–∏ –≤–∑–¥—ã–º–∞—é—â–µ–≥–æ—Å—è –≤–≤–µ—Ä—Ö –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Å–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Å—Ç–µ–Ω–∞–º–∏ –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–≥–æ –∫—Ä–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∞, –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª—É –Ω–µ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–∏. –í–æ–∫—Ä—É–≥ —à–∞—Ö—Ç—ã –±—ã–ª–∏ —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–µ —à–µ—Å—Ç—ã, –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—É—é—â–∏–µ –∫–≤–∞–¥—Ä–∞—Ç —Å–æ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–æ–π –≤ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–∫–æ–≤ –º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–≤, –∞ –Ω–∞ –Ω–∏—Ö –±—ã–ª–∞ –Ω–∞—Ç—è–Ω—É—Ç–∞ —Å–µ—Ç–∫–∞ –∏–∑ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ–ª–æ–∫–∏ –∏–ª–∏ —Ç—Ä–æ—Å–∞. –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ —è—á–µ–π–∫–∏ —Å–µ—Ç–∫–∏ –∑–∞–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–¥–º–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä–æ–º —Å –µ–≥–æ —Ç–µ–ª–æ. –ö–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, —ç—Ç—É —Å–µ—Ç–∫—É –ø–æ–∑–∞–∏–º—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–ª–∏ –∏–∑ —Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∑–∞–ª–∞, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—â–µ–≥–æ—Å—è –¥–ª—è –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –∏–≥—Ä—ã —Å –º—è—á–æ–º –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–≥–æ —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä–∞.
–°—Ç–æ—è—â–∏–µ –≤–æ–∫—Ä—É–≥ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä—ã —Ç–∏—Ö–æ —Å—Ç–æ–Ω–∞–ª–∏ –∏ —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø–µ–ª–∏, –ø—Ä–∏–≤—ã–∫–∞—è –∫ –∫–æ—Å–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–º—É —Ö–æ–ª–æ–¥—É –∏ –≤–∞–∫—É—É–º—É, –æ–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –ª—é–¥–∏ –≤ –Ω–∏—Ö, –∑–∞–Ω—è—Ç—ã–µ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º–∏ –¥–µ–ª–∞–º–∏, –ø–æ—Ö–æ–∂–µ, —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞–ª–∏. –ú–∞–π–∫–ª –ø–æ—à–µ–≤–µ–ª–∏–ª—Å—è, –∏ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª –æ—Ç–∫–ª–∏–∫–Ω—É–ª—Å—è –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ —Å–ª–∞–±—ã–º –ø–æ—Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –≤ –∑–≤—É–∫–æ–≤–æ–º –¥–∏–∞–ø–∞–∑–æ–Ω–µ.
–ú–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫ —Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª –æ–± —ç—Ç–æ–º –¥–æ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –ô–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏ –∏ –ø–æ–ø—ã—Ç–∞–ª—Å—è –≤–ø–∏—Ç–∞—Ç—å –≤ —Å–µ–±—è –µ–≥–æ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–µ–≤–Ω—è—Ç–Ω—ã–π –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç, —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è—â–∏–π –∏–∑ –º–∞—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É–ª, –ø—Ä–∏–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—Å–∏—Ö–æ–ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ —Ç–µ—Ä–º–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏. –ë—ã—Ç—å –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç, —Å–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–µ–º, –∑–∞–∫–æ–Ω—á–∏–≤ —à–∫–æ–ª—É, –æ–Ω –Ω–∞—É—á–∏—Ç—Å—è —Ä–∞–∑–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –≤ –ø–æ–¥–æ–±–Ω—ã—Ö –≤–µ—â–∞—Ö. –ü–æ–∫–∞ –∂–µ, —Å—É–¥—è –ø–æ –≤—Å–µ–º—É, –ª—É—á—à–µ –ø–æ–ø—ã—Ç–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç —Å–∞–º–æ–º—É.
‚Äì –í—ã –≥–æ—Ç–æ–≤—ã? ‚Äì –ö –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫—É –ø—Ä–∏–±–ª–∏–∑–∏–ª—Å—è –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–π –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Å–∫–∞—Ñ–∞–Ω–¥—Ä –¢—É–ø–µ–ª–æ–≤–∞. –ú–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä —Å —Å–∞–º–æ–≥–æ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–∞ –æ–±—Ä–∞—â–∞–ª—Å—è –∫ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª—É —Å —É–≤–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º, –∫–∞–∫ –∫ —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ–º—É.
–ï—â–µ –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ –≤–Ω–∏–∑—É –æ–±–ª–∞—á–∞–ª–∏ –≤ —è—Ä–∫–æ-–æ—Ä–∞–Ω–∂–µ–≤—ã–π –æ–±–ª–µ–≥–∞—é—â–∏–π —Å–ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ—Å—Ç—é–º, –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ —Ç–µ–º –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞–¥–µ—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ–≥–æ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª, –µ–º—É –≤–∫—Ä–∞—Ç—Ü–µ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É –∏—Å–ø—ã—Ç–∞–Ω–∏–π –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–≥–æ–¥–Ω—è: –æ–Ω –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–∏—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–±–æ–¥–Ω—ã–π –ø–æ–ª–µ—Ç –≤ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ. –ù–µ —É—Å–ø–µ–ª –ú–∞–π–∫–ª —Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞ –ø–æ–¥—É–º–∞—Ç—å –æ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—á–∏–∫–∏ —Å–ø–µ—à–∞—Ç, –∫–∞–∫ –±–∞–∑–∞–ª—å—Ç–æ–≤—É—é –ø–ª–æ—â–∞–¥–∫—É –∑–∞–ª–∏–ª –æ—Å–ª–µ–ø–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π —Å–≤–µ—Ç. –ü—Ä–æ—à–ª–æ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –º–≥–Ω–æ–≤–µ–Ω–∏–π, –ø—Ä–µ–∂–¥–µ —á–µ–º ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç¬ª –æ—Å–ª–∞–±–∏–ª —Ä–∞–¥–∏–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –∏–∑–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –ø—Ä–µ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—É–µ–º–æ–µ –≤ –≤–∏–¥–∏–º—ã–π —Å–ø–µ–∫—Ç—Ä –∏ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–≤–∞–µ–º–æ–µ –Ω–µ–ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–µ—Ç—á–∞—Ç–∫—É –≥–ª–∞–∑–∞. –î–∞, —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –≤–µ–¥—É—Ç—Å—è –≤ —Å–ø–µ—à–∫–µ, –Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –±—ã—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω—ã, –∏ –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω—ã –≤–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ. –ù–∏ –¢—É–ø–µ–ª–æ–≤, –Ω–∏ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–µ —Å—Ç–∞–ª–∏ –±—ã –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞—Å–Ω–æ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–∏–º –¥–µ—Ç–∏—â–µ–º.
–û–±—Å–ª—É–∂–∏–≤–∞–≤—à–∏–µ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª–∞ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–∏–∫–∏ —Å–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω –ø—Ä–∏–ª–∞–∂–∏–≤–∞–ª–∏ –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–Ω–µ–Ω—Ç—ã ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç–∞¬ª. –≠—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–∏ –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏—Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤ –≤–∏–¥–µ –∫—É–±–∏–∫–æ–≤. –û–Ω–∏ –±–µ—Å—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–æ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–∞–ª–∏ –ø–æ–¥ —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫–∞–º–∏ ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç–∞¬ª, –Ω–∏—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–µ —É–≤–µ–ª–∏—á–∏–≤–∞—è –Ω–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫—É –Ω–∞ –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫–∞.
–ú–∞–π–∫–ª –Ω–∞ –º–∏–Ω—É—Ç—É –æ—Ç–≤–ª–µ–∫—Å—è. –ß–µ—Ç—ã—Ä—å–º—è —ç—Ç–∞–∂–∞–º–∏ –Ω–∏–∂–µ –∏ –≤ –¥–≤–µ–Ω–∞–¥—Ü–∞—Ç–∏ –∫–∏–ª–æ–º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö –∫ –ª—É–Ω–Ω–æ–º—É –∑–∞–ø–∞–¥—É –µ–≥–æ –º–∞—Ç—å –æ–∂–∏–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –±–æ–ª—Ç–∞–ª–∞ —Å –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –¥–∞–º–æ–π, –≤–∏—Ü–µ-–ø—Ä–µ–∑–∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º –ê–∫–∞–¥–µ–º–∏–∏. –ö–∞—Ä–º–µ–Ω —Å–æ—á–ª–∞ —Å—á–∞—Å—Ç–ª–∏–≤–æ–π —Å–ª—É—á–∞–π–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é, —á—Ç–æ –æ—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å –ê–∫–∞–¥–µ–º–∏–∏, –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â–∏–π, –æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª—Å—è –Ω–∞ –õ—É–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ë–∞–∑–µ –∏ –Ω–∞—à–µ–ª –≤—Ä–µ–º—è —Å –Ω–µ–π –ø–æ–±–µ—Å–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å‚Ä¶
–î–æ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –ô–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏–ª –≤ –º–∏–∫—Ä–æ—Ñ–æ–Ω, —Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä—É—è —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –Ω–∞ –º–∞–≥–Ω–∏—Ç–æ—Ñ–æ–Ω–µ:
‚Äì –°–µ–≥–æ–¥–Ω—è –º—ã –Ω–∞—á–Ω–µ–º —Å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–∏–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ-–æ—Ç–ª–∏–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ –Ω–∞–∫–æ–ø–∏—Ç–µ–ª—è –≤ —Ñ–æ—Ä—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–µ. –ú—ã –±—É–¥–µ–º –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è –¥–ª—è –º–∞–Ω–µ–≤—Ä–æ–≤ —ç–Ω–µ—Ä–≥–∏—é –∞–∫–∫—É–º—É–ª—è—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≤. –ù–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–æ–º —ç—Ç–∞–ø–µ –∑–∞–ø–ª–∞–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–µ–π—à–∏–µ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è. –ò—Å–ø—ã—Ç—É–µ–º—ã–π –ø–æ–¥–Ω–∏–º–µ—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞–¥ –ø–æ–≤–µ—Ä—Ö–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –Ω–∞ –¥–≤–∞-—Ç—Ä–∏ –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞, –ø–æ–¥ –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Å–µ—Ç–∫–∞–º–∏, –∞ –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–∏—Ç —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ–º—É—é –ø–æ—Å–∞–¥–∫—É. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —Ç–æ–≥–æ –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–∞ —Å—Ç–∞–¥–∏—è –∏—Å–ø—ã—Ç–∞–Ω–∏—è –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞, –º—ã –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ —Ä–µ—à–∏–º, —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ.
–ú–∞–π–∫–ª —É—Å–ø–µ–ª –≤—ã—è—Å–Ω–∏—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ —É ¬´–õ–∞–Ω—Å–µ–ª–æ—Ç–∞¬ª –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç—Å—è –∑–∞–ø–∞—Å–Ω—ã–π –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫ —ç–Ω–µ—Ä–≥–∏–∏, —Ç–µ—Ä–º–æ—è–¥–µ—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä, –Ω–∞ –≤–∑–≥–ª—è–¥ –º–∞–ª—å—á–∏–∫–∞, —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—Ä–æ–º –≤ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ä–∞–∑ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ, —á–µ–º —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–ª–æ—Å—å. –≠—Ç–æ—Ç —Ä–µ–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª—Å—è –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ –≤ –ø–æ–ª—É–ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–∫–ª–∞–¥–∫–∞—Ö –º–µ–∂–¥—É –µ–≥–æ –ª–æ–ø–∞—Ç–∫–∞–º–∏, –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∞—Ö –≤ –¥–≤—É—Ö –æ—Ç —Å–ø–∏–Ω—ã. –£—á–µ–Ω—ã–µ –æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏–ª–∏, —á—Ç–æ –≤ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç–æ—è—â–∏–π –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –æ–Ω —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –≤ –∫–≤–∞–∑–∏–º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–µ: –º–æ–ª–µ–∫—É–ª—ã –±—ã–≤—à–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ —Ç–≤–µ—Ä–¥–æ–≥–æ —É—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã –ª–∏—à—å –≤–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∞–º–∏ —Å–∏–ª. –ê —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª–æ —Å–∏–ª–∞–º–∏ –≤ –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–Ω–æ–º —Ä–µ–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–µ, —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –ø—Ä–µ–≤—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–ª–æ—Å—å –≤ –µ—â–µ –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –∞–±—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–µ –∏ –Ω–µ—É–ª–æ–≤–∏–º—ã–µ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏—Ü—ã; –Ω–æ —Ç–µ–º –Ω–µ –º–µ–Ω–µ–µ —Ç–µ—Ä–º–æ—è–¥–µ—Ä–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–∞–∫—Ç–æ—Ä –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–ª –≤—Å–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏. –ö–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ, –∫–∞–∫ —Å–∫–∞–∑–∞–ª –æ–¥–∏–Ω –∏–∑ —É—á–µ–Ω—ã—Ö, –º–∞—Ç–µ—Ä–∏—è ‚Äì —ç—Ç–æ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è–µ–º–∞—è —Ç–µ–º, –∫–∞–∫–∏–º–∏ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏ –º—ã –∏–∑–º–µ—Ä—è–µ–º –µ–µ –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–µ, –∏ –ú–∞–π–∫–ª—É –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∞–º–∏ –∫–∞–∑–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, —á—Ç–æ –∏–Ω–æ–≥–¥–∞ –µ–º—É —É–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ—â—É—Ç–∏—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ —á–µ–≥–æ-—Ç–æ –Ω–µ–æ–±—ä—è—Å–Ω–∏–º–æ–≥–æ, —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ–Ω –µ—â–µ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞—É—á–∏–ª—Å—è –¥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ü–∞ —Ä–∞–∑–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –≤ –ø–æ–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω–∏—è—Ö —Å–≤–æ–∏—Ö –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–æ–≤ —á—É–≤—Å—Ç–≤.

Trmt5 (TRM5 tRNA methyltransferase 5) - Chinchilla Research Resource Database
Gene: Trmt5 (TRM5 tRNA methyltransferase 5) Mus musculus
Description: Predicted to have tRNA (guanine-N1-)-methyltransferase activity. Predicted to be involved in mitochondrial tRNA methylation and tRNA N1-guanine methylation. Predicted to localize to the mitochondrial matrix. Human ortholog(s) of this gene implicated in combined oxidative phosphorylation deficiency. Orthologous to human TRMT5 (tRNA methyltransferase 5); INTERACTS WITH 1,2-dichloroethane; 2,3,7,8-tetrachlorodibenzodioxine; bisphenol A.
Also known as: 2610027O18Rik; KIAA1393; M1G-methyltransferase; mKIAA1393; TRM5 tRNA methyltransferase 5 homolog; tRNA (guanine(37)-N1)-methyltransferase; tRNA (guanine-N(1)-)-methyltransferase; tRNA [GM37] methyltransferase; tRNA methyltransferase 5; tRNA methyltransferase 5 homolog

Soomaaliland oo la wareegtay deegaanka Boocame oo ...
Soomaaliland oo la wareegtay deegaanka Boocame oo ay ku sugnaayeen Ciidamada Puntland | Radio Hiranweyn Somalia latest news
Home Wararka Soomaaliland oo la wareegtay deegaanka Boocame oo ay ku sugnaayeen Ciidamada Puntland
Soomaaliland oo la wareegtay deegaanka Boocame oo ay ku sugnaayeen Ciidamada Puntland
Wararka ka imaanayo deegaanka Boocame ee gobolka Sool ayaa waxaa ay sheegayaan in Ciidamo ka tirsan Soomaaliland ay lawareegeen Saldhigii deegaankaas oo ay gacanta ku hayeen Ciidamada Puntland.
Saldhiga deegaanka Boocame ayaa waxaa Ciidamada la wareegay ay yihiin Ciidamo ka tirsan kuwa maamulka Somaliland oo horey uga mid ahaa Ciidamada Booliska Puntland balse ku biirey Soomaaliland.
Ciidamadaan la wareegay Saldhiga deegaanka Boocame ee Gobolka Sool ayaa waxaa hoggaamkinaya Saraakiil Caanka ah deegaannada Puntland,waxaana la sheegay inay xerada ka taageen Calanka Soomaaliland.
Wararka ayaa waxaa ay intasi ku darayaan in Saraakiil ka tirsan Ciidamada Soomaaliland ay gaareen degaanka Boocame,kuwaas oo Gadiidka nooca dagaalka iyo Ciidamo kale ku kordhiyey Ciidamada la wareegay deegaankaas.
Si kastaba tallaabadaan ay Ciidamada soomaaliland kula wareegen saldhig ay Ciidamada Puntland ku lahaayeen deegaanka Boocame ayaa waxaa uu kusoo aadayaa xilli Puntland ay horey deegaankaas uga dhistey Saldhig ay sheegeen inay uga hortagayaan weeraro kaga yimada dhinaca Soomaaliland.

Maayarka Hargeysa oo Wareegto ku Mamnuucay Qorshey...
Maayarka Hargeysa oo Wareegto ku Mamnuucay Qorsheynta Dhulka Buuraleyda ah | Waaheen Media Group
Home Wararka Maayarka Hargeysa oo Wareegto ku Mamnuucay Qorsheynta Dhulka Buuraleyda ah
Hargeysa(Waaheen) Maayarka caasimadda Hargeysa Cabdiraxmaan Maxamuud Caydiid (Solteco) ayaa wareegto uu soo saaray ku mamnuucay qorsheynta dhulka buuraleyda ah ee ku hareeraysan magaalada.
Wareegtadan oo uu maayarku ku saxeexan yahay ayuu ku faahfaahiyay sababaha keenay inay joojiyaan qorsheynta dhulka buuraleyda ah ee ku yaalla caasimadda Hargeysa.Wareegtadaasina waxay u qornayd sidan:-
‚ÄúDuqa caasimadda Hargeysa, ahna guddoomiyaha golaha deegaanka caasimadda Hargeysa:
Markuu arkay: Sharciga maamulka gobollada iyo degmooyinka Jamhuuriyada Somaliland, qodobkiisa 12aad farqadiisa 1aad iyo 3aad ee dastuurka dalka.
Markuu ogaaday: Xeer NO:17/2001 ee qodobkiisa 7aad xubintiisa 4aad oo tilmaamaya in meelaha buuraha, sanaaga dhagaxa, boholaha iwm ee magaaladu gaadho looma aqoonsanayo beer, magdhaw laguma celinayo.
Markuu garwaaqsaday: Duqa caasimaddu ahmiyada ay buuruhu u leeyihiin qaranka iyo nabadgelyada, si loo ilaaliyo difaaca circa ee ciidamada iyo tan ilaalinta guud ee caasimadda oo ciidamo loo dejinayo.
Markuu isku qanciyay: Duqa caasimaddu ahmiyada buuruhu u leeyihiin in la dhigo toowaro ku shaqeeya tamarta laydhka, cadceeda iyo dabaysha.
Markuu tixgeliyay: Tallada masuuliyiinta ay khusayso hawshani, wuxuu soo saaray:
1- Ka dib markii uu arkay dhamaan asbaabaha kor ku xusan laga bilaabo maalintii ay bishu ahayd 26/09/2013 wuxuu go‚Äôaansaday in gabi ahaanba la joojiyay qorsheynta dhulka buuraha, marka laga reebo dhulka babaca ah ee biyo shubka beerta ah sida ku cad Xeer NO: 17/2001, qodobkiisa 7aad, xubintiisa 4aad‚Äù.

Baarlamaanka Norway oo diiday in 4-jirkan xanuunsa...
Baarlamaanka Norway oo diiday in 4-jirkan xanuunsan Norway loo soo qaado. - NorSom News
Baarlamaanka Norway oo diiday in 4-jirkan xanuunsan Norway loo soo qaado.
Foto: 2019 FREE BURMA RANGERS
Baarlamaanka Norway ayaa jimcihii lasoo dhaafay cod u qaaday in Norway loo soo qaado 4 sano jir Norwiiji ah oo xanuunsan, ayna dhaleen hooyo iyo aabe Norway ka tagay, kuna biiray Daacish.
Wiilkan 4 sano jirka ah oo xaaladiisa caafimaad laga deyrinayo, kuna sugan xeryaha qoxootiga Siiriya ayaa waxaa dhalay hooyo iyo aabe heysta dhalashada Norway, kana wada tirsanaa kooxda Daacish ee burburtay.
Hooyada dhashay cunugaas yar oo ku sugan xeryaha qoxootiga ayaa horey u codsaday in la badbaadiyo wiilkeeda oo xaaladiisa caafimaad ay kasii dareyso. Waxeyna hooyadan sidoo kale heysataa gabar kale oo wiilka xanuunsan la dhalatay.
Xisbiga MDG ayaa baarlamaanka Norway u gudbiyay mooshin codsi ah oo lagu dalbanayo in wiilkaas Norway loo soo qaado, laguna daaweeyo. Waxeyna codsadeen in xukuumada lagu cadaadiyo arintaas.
Baarlamaanka Norway ayaa jimcihii cod aqlabiyad xoogan leh ku diiday in wiilkaas Norway loo soo qaado. Waxaana mooshinkaas diiday xisbiyada Ap, Krf, Venstre, Sp, Frp iyo H√∏yre.
Xisbiyada MDG(oo mooshinka keenay), R√∏dt iyo Sv ayaana noqday sadexda xisbi ah ee kali ah ee u codeeyay in afar sano jirkaas xanuunsan Norway loo soo qaado.
Waxaa xusid mudan in horey ay dowlada Norway usoo jeedisay in wiilka xanuunsan kaligiis loo soo qaado Norway, isaga oo hooyadiis aysan la socon. Balse hooyada ayaa arintaas ku gacan seyrtay, codsadeyna in qoyskeeda oo dhameystiran lasoo wada badbaadiyo.
Xigasho/kilde: Stortinget sier nei til √• hente hjem syk fire√•ring og IS-kvinne

Next article(Xog): Muxuu salka ku hayaa khilaafka sababay in masaajidka Towfiiq laga goosto taageerada dhaqaale ee dowlada.

Gabdha Buurbuuran iyo Kuwa Caatada ah Kuwee ayaa Ku wanaagsan Dhanka Sariirta? Waxaa hubaal ah in ragu jecelyihiin gabdhaha buurbuuran caadiyan oo ay u maleeyaan inay ka helayaan raaxo aysan ka helayn gabdhaha caatada ah. haddaba gabdhaha buurbuuran iyo kuwa caatada ah kuwee ayaa dhanka sariirta ku wanaagsan. ka ogow siraha barta Shukaansiga ee shukaansi Blog.
Sida runta nin walba waxa uu ku hamiyaa inuu helo naag uu ka helayo raaxo dhamaystiran marka la joogo sariirta. raaxadaasi ha noqoto mid jireed iyo mid awood dareen.
Haddaba cimlmi baariso badan oo aan samaynay iyo kuwo ay sameeyeen khuburo caafimaad ayaa waxay ogaadeen in gabdhaha caatada ah ay ka raaxo macaanyihiin kuwa buurbuuran. siyaalaha la ogaaday inay uga raaxo badanyihiina waxaa ka mid ah.
Dumarka caatada ah badanaa waa ka dareen kululyihiin kuwa buurbuuran
Dumarka caatada ah waxay samayn karaan dhaqdhaqaaqyo aysan samayn karin kuwa buurbuuran.
Dumarka caatada ah waxay leeyihiin badanaa naaso yaryar oo ku macaan dhanka salaaxida iyo dhuuqmada.
Barida dumarka caatada ah waxay ka macaan tahay barida dumarka buurbuuran.
sidoo kale waxaa l sheegaa in dumarka caatada ah aysan marnaba ka daalayn in loo raaxeeyo halka dumarka buurbuuran ay gataati dhac noqonayaan marka laba jeer la garaaco.
lasoco qormooyin kaa caawin doona inaad heso nolol raaxo leh.
Waxaa jira waxyaalo fara badan oo qofka caafimaadkiisa jir ahaaneed u wanaagsan kuwaas oo haddii uu sameeyo u noqda go'aan fiican oo uu u aayo.
maadaama caafimaadku yahay waxa ugu horeeya ee qofka bini'aadankaa uu ka taxadaro la'aantiisna aysan suurta galayn qofku inuu anfaco nafiisa iyo bulshadiisa toona waxaa lagama maarmaan ah in caafimaadka la siiyo muhiimada koowaad, labaad iyo saddexaad.
Haddaba shantaan waxyaalood waa kuwo muhiim ah oo caafimaadkaaga taabo galinaya kana dhigaya mid sugan oo faya qabkiisu yahay heersare.
qodobadaan caafimaad ee halkaan aan idiinku soo bandhigi doono waxay sidoo kale ka sugnaadeen xaga diinta waana dawooyin la soo isticmaalay oo diinta sunne iyo qoraanka lagu soo arkay.
1. xabbad sowdada:
Wabbad sowdadu waa miro yar oo madmadow oo la cuno, la tumo oo lagu daro cabitaanka siiba shaaha ama la cabo, sidoo kale waxaa lagu milaa saliid islamakaana waa la cabaa ama la marsadaa oo lagu subkaa jirka qaybihiisa siiba madax, sanka cunaha iyo xabadka.
xagee u roontahay:
waxay u roontay qaybaha sare ee jirka iyadoo qofka kala dirirta inuu ku abuurmo caabuq, duuf, sanboor iyo quman. waxa ay aad ugu fiicantahay daweynta sanka iyo cunaha sidoo kale waxaa loo adeegsan karaa xanuunada caloosha waana dawo wanaagsan oo ka sugnaatay nabigeena. waxaa ku saaran inaad isticmaashid maadaama ay u wanaagsantahay caafimaadkaaga, caafimaadkaaguna yahay waxa ugu muhiimsan ee aad ilaashato.
Waa shay hoor ah, midab casuus ah leh oo ay samayso shinnidu ka dib marka ay soo nuugto dhirta kala duwan ubaxeeda.
waa dawo aan la isku hayn taas oo u wanaagsan xanuuno badan oo xiligan aad ugu soo badanaya wadankeena sida Dhiig karka, macaanka iyo laabjeexa. waxa kale oo uu aad wax uga taraa caloosha oo uu ka qayb qaato sifaynteeda iyo qashin saarkeeda.
waxaa sidoo kale la xaqiijiyey inuu qayb muhiim ah ka ciyaaro ilaalinta timaha luma ama jarma uuna ka hortago bidaarta degdega ah sidoo kalena uu soo celiyo timaha bidaaroobey ee waqtigooda gaarin.
waa dawo u wanaagsan caafimaadkaaga ee cun.
3. caanaha:
Caalamka qof walba oo jooga waxa uu cabaa caanaha waxay ay caanuhu ka qayb qaataan caafimaadkaaga ayagoo la dagaalama ama soo celiya unugyada ku luma shucaaca qalabka farsamada casrigaa ay sii dayaan iyo dhibaatooyinka ay keenaan shaqada iyo daalka faraha badan.
Caanuhu waxay dhisaan maskaxda waxayna ka hortagaan xanuuno badan sidoo kale waxaa muhiim ah in qofku uu la socdo inay haboontahay in ubadka lagu waraabsho caanaha inta ay yaryihiin.
4. qaraha ama xabxabka:
Qaruhu waxa uu ka qaybqaataa sifaynta iyo nadiifinta qaybta kaadi mareenka ee jirka bin aadanka isagoo si wanaagsan u xaliya dhibaatada kaadiyeed ee qofka soo food saarta, kaadida oo ah qashin aad u dhibaato badan iyo suman uu aruursahay habdhiskaasi waxaa si waafi ah jirka uga saara waa qaraha. si caafimaadka kaadi mareenkaagu u noqdo mid wanaagsan fadlan qaraha badso.
5. basha iyo toonta:
Waa labo shay oo qaali ah kuwaas oo waxtara dheecaanka u dhexeeya lafaha si wanaagsana u soo celiya. maadaama ay yihiin geed kulay waxa kale oo ay la dagaalamaan hargabka iyo waxyaalaha ay soo waaridaan dabaysa iyo dhaxant.
Caafimaadkaaga ka taxadar oo ilaasho waa adiga waxa aad qiimo ku leedahay caafimaadku ee ha moodin inaad caafimaad la'aan naftaada iyo cid kale toona aad wax taraysid.
Waxaa jira waxyaalo badan oo dadka caafimaadkooda, waxsoosaarkooda iyo firfircoonidooda hoos u dhiga si baaxad leh.
haddaba halkaan ayaan idinku soo gudbinaynaa saddexda ugu daran ee wax u dhima noloshaada.
1. balwada:
waxaa ugu caansan Xashiishka, Qaadka, Sigaarka iwm waa shayga koowaad ee naftaada baabi'iya waxa uuna kugu abuuraa.
- xushmadaada oo baaba'da
- noloshaada oo is bedesha
- caafimaadkaaga oo xumaada
iyo waxyaalo kale oo aan lasoo koobi karin.
waxaana soo jeedin ahaan usoo jeedinaynaa si loo helo farxad dhamaystiran mid gaar ah iyo mid qoysba in laga fogaado waxyaalaha balwada ah.
2. daryeel la'aanta nafta:
waxaa ugu horeeya soo jeedka badan cunto qaab daran oo aad cuntid, taxadar la'aanteeda, nadaafada oo aadan daryeelin iyo adigoo badsada wax alaale iyo wixii dhibaato kuu keeni kara.
3. haddalka xun:
haddalka xumi waxa uu kuu soo jiidaa dhibaatin badan iyo tacadiyo nafeed oo badan waxaa ku karaahsanaya bulshada waxaana ku haleelaya cuduro baaxad leh oo aadan garanayn waxa ay yihiin.
haddaba ka fogow intaanba adigoo ku bedelanaya, ciyaaraha, jimicsiga, waanada, la talinta.
1. daacadnimo: ma jirto wax ka qaalisan oo lagu farxo lamaane daacad kuu ah markaasna ka shaqaynay sidii aad u higsan lagayd horumarka aad ka damacsantahay nolosha.
3. qalbi furnaan: guriga lamaanaha ku nooli haday kala aaminsanyihiin waxyaalo keeni kara aamusnaan, baqdin iyo canaan waxaa dawo u noqon kara in labada ruux ay isu muujiyaan qalbi furnaan iyo kalgacayl.
5. nadaafad: bilnaanta jir ahaaneed, guri ahaaneed iyo muuqaal wanaagsan waxay kordhiyaan oo kor u qaadaan xubiga iyo wanaaga ay isku hayaan labada lamaane, waxaana soo ifbaxaya udgoonka iyo quruxda ay leedahay nolosha lamaanaha ah.
galabtii markii la gaaro guda gal hagaajinta iyo nadiifinta jirkaag adiga oo ka bilaabaya ilkahaaga kuna xiginaya jirka intiisa kale ku qabayso biyo aab kulalayn sidoo kale isticmaal waxyaalaha jirka lagu nadiifiyo sida saabuun shaamboo iwm ha ilaawin in aad cuntid waxyaalo cunto fudud ah oo u badan qudaar iyo hal koob oo qaxweah maqribka marka la gaaro qaado casho wanaagsan -hadaad ninka tahay guriga agagaarkiisa iska layrso, -hadaad gabadha tahay markaas waxaa kuu yaala shaqo aad u fara badan qabays gaaban qaado ka dibna sariirtaad ama qolkaaga iska sii tag adiga oo udug aad us sareeya isticmaalaya isla markaana ku mashquulaya kala bixinta jirkaaga iyo timahaaga

XOG: Mukhtaar Roobow oo Halis ku jira iyo Isbitaaa...
XOG: Mukhtaar Roobow oo Halis ku jira iyo Isbitaaalka Digfeer oo la geeyay | Hobyo Media Online
Home Arimaha Bulshada XOG: Mukhtaar Roobow oo Halis ku jira iyo Isbitaaalka Digfeer oo la...
XOG: Mukhtaar Roobow oo Halis ku jira iyo Isbitaaalka Digfeer oo la geeyay
Waxaa laga deyrinayaa xaaladda Caafimaad ee Sheekh Mukhtaar Roobow Cali Abuu Mansuur oo muddo ka badan 6 bil u xiran dowladda Soomaaliya kadib markii uu ka qeyb galay doorashada Koonfur Galbeed oo ay ka diidaneed dowladda Soomaaliya.Advertisement
Sheekh Mukhtaar Roobow ayaa habeen hore laga soo saaray Isbitaalka Digfeer ee magaalada Muqdisho halkaas oo uu ku qaatay muddo 5 habeen, sida ay xaqiijiyeen qaar kamid ah Shaqaalaha Isbitaalka iyo eheladiisa.
Abuu Mansuur ayaa ka xanuunsanaya Kiliyaha waxaana la sheegay in uu aad u dhamaaday islamarkaana ay ka sii dareyso xaaladda Caafimaad. Dhaqaatiirta Isbitaalka Digfeer ayaa ku taliyay in Sheekh Mukhtaar loo qaado dibadda si loogu soo daweeyo.
Dhaqtarka gaarka ah ee Abuu Mansuur ayaa Saraakiil katirsan Dowladda Soomaaliya kula taliyay in Sheekha loo qaado dibadda maadaama adagtahay in dalka wax looga qabto.Advertisement
Sheekh Mukhtaar Roobow oo habeen hore saqdii dhexe laga soo saaray Isbitaalka Digfeer ayaa lagu celiyay xarunta hey‚Äôadda Nabad Sugidda Soomaaliya ee Habar-khaadiijo waxaana la filayaa in dhowaan loo qaado Isbitaal ku yaalo magaalada Jeddah ee dalka Boqortooyada Sacuudi Carabiya.
Waa markii labaad muddo ka yar 40 cesho Isbitaal la dhigo Abuu Mansuur oo kaliyaha ka xanuunsanaya mana jirto ilaa hadda wax dedaal oo socda oo lagu sii deynayo Sheekh Mukhtaar Roobow Cali. Bartimihii ramadaanka ayaa sidoo kale Roobow la dhigay Isbitalka.Advertisement
Isbitaalka Digfeer ee magaalada Muqdisho, waa xarunta Caafimaad ee ugu weyn magaalada Muqdisho iyo qaar kamid ah wadamada Gobalka, hadii wax looga qaban waayyana waxaa loo badaniyaa in loo qaado wadamada dibadda.
Mukhtaar Roobow, waa adag tahay in dal walba loo qaado sida wadamada Caafimaadka ku wanaagsan sida Hindiya iyo Germany balse waxaa la filayaa in loo qaado Boqortooyada Sacuudi Carabiya iyo dalka Qatar oo aad u taageera Soomaaliya.

Xilliga uu furmayo kalfadhiga 6-aad ee Golaha Shac...

Home Photos Xilliga uu furmayo kalfadhiga 6-aad ee Golaha Shacabka oo la shaaciyay
Xilliga uu furmayo kalfadhiga 6-aad ee Golaha Shacabka oo la shaaciyay
Muqdisho ‚Äì Guddoonka Baarlamaanka Federaalka Soomaaliya ayaa maanta shaaciyay waqtiga uu furmayo kalfadhiga 6-aad ee Golaha Shacabka.
Warqad uu soo saaray Guddoomiyaha Baarlamaanka Federaalka Soomaaliya Maxamed Mursal Sheikh Cabdiraxmaan ayaa lagu sheegay in kalfadhiga 6-aad ee Baarlamaanka Federalka si ramsi uu u furmi doono 9 bishaan Ocktoobar oo ku beegan maalin Arbaco ah.
Xoghayaha Guud ee Golaha Shacabka Cabdikariim Xaaji Cabdi Buux ayaa qoraalka ka soo xaafiiska Guddoomiyaha akhriyay ayaa ugu baaqay xildhibaannada Golaha Shacabka in ay sida ugu dhaqsiyaha badan ay dalka ugu soo laabtaan si aay u gutaan waajibaadka saaran.
Golaha Baarlamaanka ayaa fasaxiisa caadiga ahaa ku jiray muddo labo bil ah iyadoo intii Xildhibaannadda ay fasaxa ku jireen ay dhaceen arrimo xasaasiya oo dhanka siyaasadda ah sida doorashooyinka Barlamaanka iyo Madaxweynaha ee Jubbaland.

IFTIINKACUSUB.COM: Qisso yaab leh:Fariin Aakhiro i...
IFTIINKACUSUB.COM: Qisso yaab leh:Fariin Aakhiro iiga timi !
Komputarkayga markii aan furay,waxa aan arkay warqad iiga timi Aakhiro,taasi oo uu iisoo diray saxiibkaygii dhawaan geeriyooday.Wakhti kasta oo aad firaaqo hayso waxa aad jeceshahay in aad furato Computarkaga , adigoo raba warar amma barnamijyo adiga kuu gaar ah in aad ka fiirsato amma aad ka akhrisato
Adiga oo soo daalay isla markasina yimi Gurigaagii amma Xafiiskagii kuu gaarka ahaa ,markii aad fadhiisatay ,ma laactay oo ma soo qabsatay Konputarkagii adiga oo donaya in aad danahaga ku fushato.
Runtii waa Sheeko layaable , haddii aad u kuur gasho waxa aad dareemaysaa in qofkasta shaqada iyo camalka uu Aduunka intuu joogay uu hayay ay Akhirana kaga horayso.
W/Q: /Khadar Ibrahim Aar.

Gudoomiyihii garabka dhalinyarada xisbiga waddani ...
Gudoomiyihii garabka dhalinyarada xisbiga waddani Maxamed Sidiiq Dhamme ayaa sheegay inuu ka tegay jagadii uu hayey kadib markii wakhtigii ka dhamaaday.
Maxamed Sidiiq Dhame ayaa lagu tilmaamaa dhalinyaradii ugu mayalka adkayd ee xisbigaasi ka tirsanayd, culayso la saaray iyo dhinacyo badan oo lagasoo maray oo ay mararka qaar ku jirtay xadhig may bedelin fikradiisii.
‚ÄúHoggaamintu waa qori isu dhiib, waxaan hoggaaminaayay dhallinyarada Xisbiga WADDANI shan sandood muddo xileedkii nala doortay wuu dhammaaday waxaana banneeyay saaka xafiiska dhallinyarada. Si hoggaan cusub loo doorto oo aanu u ilaalinno xeerka Xisbiga, dimuqraadiyada iyo in isbedel dhaco, waxaanu wareejinaynaa xafiiska dhallinyarada Xisbiga WADDANI.
Waxaan diyaar u ahay kaalin kasta oo aan u arko in aan buuxin karo Xisbiga, xisbinimaduna waa mabda‚Äô iyo aaminaad aragti hoggaamineed. Waxaan u mahadcelinayaa qof kasta oo muddada na garab istaagay, waxaanan soo dhaweynayaa dhallinyarada Xisbiga ee leh hanka iyo hoggaaminta , waxaan soo jeedinayaa in la ilaaliyo midnimada, wadajirka iyo isku duubnaanta.‚Äù
Maxamed Sadiiq dhame.

Home WARARKA Madaxweyne Farmaajo oo ka tacsiyeeyay...
Home WARARKA Madaxweyne Farmaajo oo ka tacsiyeeyay geerida Amb. Maxamed Warsame Cali Kiimiko
Madaxweyne Farmaajo oo ka tacsiyeeyay geerida Amb. Maxamed Warsame Cali Kiimiko
Madaxweynaha Soomaaliya Maxamed Cabdullaahi Farmaajo ayaa ka tacsiyeeyay geerida ku timid Amb. Maxamed Warsame Cali Kiimiko oo xalay ku geeriyoodey magaalada Nairobi.
Alle ha u naxariistee Amb. Maxamed Warsame Cali Kiimiko waxa uu ka mid ahaa aasaasayaashii iyo Madaxweynihii ugu horreeyey ee Maamulka Galmudug, isaga oo sidoo kalena Danjire ka soo noqday dalalka Faransiiska, Maraykanka iyo Qaramada Midoobey.
‚ÄúInnaa Lilaahi Wa Innaa Ilayhi Raajicuun. Aniga oo ku hadlaya magacayga iyo kan Qaranka, waxaan tacsi tiiraanyo leh u diraaya guud ahaan shacabka Soomaaliyeed, gaar ahaanna eheladii iyo qaraabadii uu ka geeriyoodey Alle ha u naxariistee Amb. Maxamed Warsame Cali.‚Äù
‚ÄúAmb. Maxamed Warsame Cali waxa uu ahaa shakhsi aqoon, karti, hufnaan iyo daacadnimo ku suntanaa. Waxa uu qayb wakhtigiisa kamid ah ku qaatay u adeegidda shacabka Soomaaliyeed isaga oo danjire ka noqday dalal badan. Sidoo kale, Marxuumku waxa uu kamid ahaa aasaasayaashii Maamulka Galmudug. Waxaan Alle ka baryayaa in uu u naxariisto oo hoygiisa ka yeello Jannatul Firdowsa, ehelkii iyo qoyskii uu ka baxayna samir iyo iimaan ka siiyo.‚Äù

Dhanaasree mehlaa ...
Abril 20, 2008,Domingo,4:30 AM.
Dhanaasree mehlaa 1 ghar 2 asatpadee-aa (685-11)
ik-oNkaar satgur parsaad. gur saagar ratnee bharpooray. amrit sant chugeh nahee dooray. har ras chog chugeh parabh bhaavai. sarvar meh hans paraanpat paavai. 1 ki-aa bag bapurhaa chhaprhee naa-ay. keecharh doobai mail na jaa-ay. 1 rahaa-o. rakh rakh charan Dharay veechaaree. dubiDhaa chhod bha-ay nirankaaree. mukat padaarath har ras chaakhay. aavan jaan rahay gur raakhay. 2 sarvar hansaa chhod na jaa-ay. paraym bhagat kar sahj samaa-ay. sarvar meh hans hans meh saagar. akath kathaa gur bachnee aadar. 3 sunn mandal ik jogee baisay. naar na purakh kahhu ko-oo kaisay. taribhavan jot rahay liv laa-ee. sur nar naath sachay sarnaa-ee. 4 aanand mool anaath aDhaaree. Gurmukh bhagat sahj beechaaree. bhagat vachhal bhai kaatanhaaray. ha-umai maar milay pag Dhaaray. 5 anik jatan kar kaal santaa-ay. maran likhaa-ay mandal meh aa-ay. janam padaarath dubiDhaa khovai. aap na cheenas bharam bharam rovai. 6 kahta-o parh-ta-o sunta-o ayk. Dheeraj Dharam DharneeDhar tayk. jat sat sanjam ridai samaa-ay. cha-uthay pad ka-o jay man patee-aa-ay. 7 saachay nirmal mail na laagai. gur kai sabad bharam bha-o bhaagai. soorat moorat aad anoop. naanak jaachai saach saroop. 81
Domingo, 7¬∫ Vaisaakh (Samvat 540 Nanakshahi) (P√°gina: 685)
Publicado por SIKH DHARMA BHAIBANDI en 9:04

Hortii Waanu Cabi Jirnay Biyaha ! Waxa Qoray Samat...
Hortii Waanu Cabi Jirnay Biyaha ! Waxa Qoray Samatar Wayab
Thursday August 09, 2018 - 15:27:42 in Maqaallo by Wariye Tiriko
Sidan wada ogsoonahay biyuhu waa nolosha nolushuna waa biyaha la,aantood waa dhimasho hadaba sidaas oo ay tahay Ayaan qaar ka mid ah xaafadaha Hargeisa ayna dhariga waxay ku saartaan ayna haysan .
Hadaba tan iyo intii uu xukumada majaraha u qabtay muuse biixi cabdi oo uu noqday madaxweynahaoo shacabku rajo badan ka naawilayeen isna lahaayeen manta ayuunbay soo noolaatay rajadiinii in aad mar uun cabi doontaan biyo macaan oo geed deeble ka yimaada balse way ka dartay oo markii horayba dhaantay .
Hargeisa oo ah caasimada Somaliland waxa ku nool in ka badan milyan Ayaan hadaba wax biyaa cabin badankoodu balse intii muuse hortii cabi jiraty ay weyday maqaalkaygan waxaan qalinka ugu qaatay in aan inyar idinla wadaago hooyo ka mid ah hooyooyinka Somaliland ahna kuwa inta badan dhibta reerku ku dhacdo ama biyo ha la doono ama wax kale oo asaaska nolosha ahba ha loo baahdee ayaa iyadoo maalin maalmaha ka mid ah cataabaysa oo calaacalaysa aan arkay ,hadaba hoyadan waxay dhabarka ku sidaa jirkaan 20 litir qaad oo ay meel durugsan ka soo xanbaartay qiyaastii taas oon ka gartay wajigeedii markii aan arkay daalka hiin faadhka iyo neef tuurka ka muuqda hooyadan Ayaan damqaday oon is idhi ka qaad oon ku idhi ken hooyo aan kaa qaadi markaas ayay naxariistii hooyo lagu yaqaanay ileene tidhi iska daa hooyo yaanu ku wasakhayne ciil weynaa !!!!
Balse waan ka diiday oo waan sii qaaday oo ilaa waxa u hadhsanaa meel laba boqol oo talaabo u jirta intii aan isa sii waraysanaynay ayay ii sheegtay in ilaa intaa muuse biixi uu madaxweynaha ahaa aanay biyaba cabin waxayna tidhi " hooyo kaanu islahayn waxbuu idiin qaban oo waa idin noolayn sawka ilaahay sidaas u gartay markuu madaxweynaha noqday ayayba goyeen waxaan kala garan waayay inay isaga ku xumaynayaan iyo in ay ogaan ka tahay walaahi waa yaab waxaas oo roob ah ayaa da,ay maalmihii u danbeeyay balse dhibiq biyo ah kama arag markii hore oo ninkii hore mareeyaha joogay nin wanaagsan ayuu ahaa oo markaan u cabano waa soo dayn jiray balse imika ku yar oo is daawanaya oo meel kale awood ka haysta garan waynay ayaa haysta oo markaa u cabanaba noo hanjabaya , hadaba iyadoo hadalkeedii ii sii wada ayay ii sheegtay in meel halkan ah oo gurigeeda u dhaw in niman tujaar ah lacag bixiyeen oo biyo qaybiyaha siyeen oo biyihii loo sii daayay waa siday hadalka u dhigtee markii aan weydiiyayna waxay tidhi hooyo ciradaas Ayaan leeyahee ma been Ayaan sheegi karaa qolo soo aragtay waxay ii sheegeen in reero halkeer ah oon cabi jirinba inay imika cabaan hadaba cabaar markii aan soo sheekaysanaynay ayaan gaadhnay gurigeedii markii ayay ducu ugu hurgufday hadaba arintan waxay dhaxalsiisay weydiino badan islaantu ma ogayn waxa aan ahay ana iyada ma aqaan balse waxan markiiba is weydiiyay in manta umada sidaas u taal daran qofka dhibaya eek u jees jeesaya halkuu ilaahay ka gali doono sidoo kale waxaan la yaabay in manta madaxweynuhu iska arki waayo jalaafooyinka iyo qardoofaha lala maagan yahay xukumadiisa oo ah in shacabka lagu diri hadab sida ay sheegaan culimada wax ka qorta xaalada dunida ayaa sheega in dagaalka saddexaad aduunku ka dhici doono biyaha wallow Somaliland lagu daro wadamada ugu biyaha badan Ayaan hadana biyo la,aantaasna ka taagan tahay hadaba waxaan soo jeedinayaa
In madaxweynuhu u dhug yeesho waxyaabaha isaga wiiqaya , In Lala Xisaabtamo hayadaha sida wakaalada biyaha oo ah tan gabtay shaqadeediioo lays odhan karo waa gaabis
Samatar wayab
Ba . international relation and diplomacy
Journalist , and political analysis

amiirsamo@gmail.com

Istiingrey
Uumamni kunStingrayjedhama. Stingray Sanyii qurxummiiti. Qaamni uumama kanaatis kan ajaa‚Äôibaati. Qaamni isaa akka eelee biddeenaa ykn ammoo akka sahanii midhaan irratti nyaannu diriiraadha. Garuu akka eelee fi sahanii san gabaabaa miti. Qurxummiin kun bishaan oowwa qabu filata. Akkasumas bishaan akkaan gad dhooqatu keessa, lafatti gad dhihaatee jiraata. Sanyiin uumama kanaa hanga 60 akka ta‚Äôus qorannoodhaan bira gahamee jira. Sanyiin jahatamman kunniin guddina, bocaa fi amala garagaraa qabu.
Stingray qurxummii guddaadha. Qurxummiin kun haga meetira 2 lafarra dheerata. ulfaatinni isaa Kg 360 ni gaha. Qaama hagana bal‚Äôatuu fi ulfaatu keessa lafeen hin jiru. Haa ta‚Äôu malee wanti akka lafeetti tajaajilu qaama isaa keessatti argama. Kunis sanyiiwwan Shaarkii hedduun isa wal fakkeessa. Sanyiileen qurxummii kan akka shaarkii fi Stingray qaama cartilage jedhamutu akka lafeetti isaan tajaajila. Qaamni akka lafee kan kaartileejii irraa ijaarame kun qaama keenya keessattis ni argama. Qaama keenya keessaa funyaanii fi gurri kaartileejii irraa ijaarame. Haaluma wal fakkaatuun stingray qaama isaa keessaa wanti akka lafeetti isa tajaajilu, jabinni isaa akkuma funyaanii fi gurra keenyaa jira jechudha.
Qaamni qurxummii kanaa bal‚Äôaa fi diriiraan kun gama duubaatii ammoo eegee dheeraa qaba. Eegeen isaa kun wantoota qara qabanii fi summii of keessaa qaba. Eegee qara qabu kana summii wajjiin walitti dabalee diina isa adamsuuf dhufu ofirraa ittiin ittisa. Summii isaa kanaan bineensota gurguddoo heddu ajjeesuu ni danda‚Äôa. Doktorooni bara qaroomina Griikii durii turan, summii isaa kana xiqqeessanii fayyadamuudhaan, ilma namaa wal‚Äôaanuuf akka dawaa qaama hadoochuutti fayyadamaa turan.
Namoonni hedduun qurxummii kana ajjeesanii eegee isaa irraa, albee fi meeshaa waraanaa garagaraa hojjatan. Stingray du‚Äôus summiin isaa yeroo dheeraaf turuu danda‚Äôa. kanaafuu du‚Äôee jira jedhanii itti dhihaachuun rakkina guddaaf nama saaxiluu danda‚Äôa. Ijji qurxummii kana gama gubbaa qaama isaa irratti argama. Haa ta‚Äôu malee diina isaa ittiin ofirraa laaluuf ykn ammoo soorata barbaadatuuf ija isaatti hin fayyadamu. Bakka san waan electro sensor jedhamu qaba. Electro sensorri kanaan chaarjiiwwan uumama biraa irraa bishaan keessatti gad dhiifaman sensegodhee, Diina yoo ta‚Äôe jalaa dheessa. Yoo soorata ta‚Äôe ammoo saffisaan itti dhaqee adamsa. Qurxummiin kun Hedduminaan uumamaalee shrimp jedhaman soorata. Afaan isaa ammoo gara jalaatiin argama. Soorata argates irga jabaa qabutti fayyadamee caccabsee soorata.
Akkaataan uumamni kun bishaan keessa daakus kan ajaa‚Äôibaati. Yeroo uumama kana bishaan keessatti argitan waan allaattiin bishaan jala lixxee daakaa jirtu isinitti fakkaata. Qaama isaa bal‚Äôaa san gama fiixee isaa akkuma allaattii olii fi gad sochoosaa bishaan keessa daaka. Uumamni kun hedduminaan kopha kophaa jiraata. Yeroo tokko tokko qofa walitti dhufa. Stingray hoosiftoota keessatti ramadama. Kanaafuu fakkaattii isaa dhala jechuudha. Yeroo takkaan ilmoolee hanga 6 dhaluu danda‚Äôa. ilmooleen dhalatan kunniin guyyama dhalatan san of danda‚Äôu. Sooratas yeroma san barbaadatanii sooratu. Jireenya kopha kophaatis yeroma san jalqabu.
Akkuma ofii isaaniitii soorata baraadatanii sooratan, isaanillee uumama hedduuf akka soorataatti tajaajilu. Dabalataanis ilmi namaa eegee isaanii qara qabu san akkasumas summii isaanii sanitti waan haajamuuf adamsee ajjeesa. Sababa kanaaf hedduminaan bishaan qilee keessa gadi fagaatanii jiraatu. Bifti qaama isaanii cirrachaa fi biqiltoota garagaraa bishaan keessa jiraniin waan wal fakkaatuuf, diinni isaan adamsu haala salphaan argachuu hin danda‚Äôu jechuudha.

XISBIGA WADANI OO TAHLI KARIWAAYEY INUU SHACABKII ...
XISBIGA WADANI OO TAHLI KARIWAAYEY INUU SHACABKII SOO DOORTAY LA WADAAGO DHIBTA IYO GUDOOMIYAHA WADANI OO KHASNADII GOLAHA WAKIILADA KU TAKRI FALAYA | Dhamays Media Group
XISBIGA WADANI OO TAHLI KARIWAAYEY INUU SHACABKII SOO DOORTAY LA WADAAGO DHIBTA IYO GUDOOMIYAHA WADANI OO KHASNADII GOLAHA WAKIILADA KU TAKRI FALAYA
Xisbiga Wadani Oo Tahli Kariwaayey Inuu Shacabkii Soo Doortay La Wadaago Dhibta Iyo Gudoomiyaha Wadani Oo Khasnadii Golaha Wakiilada Ku Takri Falaya.
Dalkeena somaliland waxaa uu xiligan ku jiraa marxalad abaareed oo adag taasi oo sabab u noqotay in la waayo duunyo badan oo xoolo u badan halka qaar kamida deeganada galbeedka somaliland dad ugu dhinteen gaajo ay sababtay abaarta iyo macaluusha baahsan ee jirata hadaba iyadoo dadkeenu gurmad u baahan yihiin ayaa jira in Xisbiga Curdinkaa ee Wadani oo isagu ku cusub saaxada siyaasada islamarkaana fadhi barad ah uu xigan ku foogan yahay inuu ku tagri faloo .
Ma nasiib xumo ka weyn ba jirta marka aad garan waydo hadba marxalada kula gudboon gudoomiyaha wadani wuxuu garan la,ayahay talaabada la gudboon iyadoo shacabkiisii uu codkooda ku fadhiyey marna xisbigiisa kusoo saaray inuu garan waayo dareenka abaareed iyo xaalada cakiran ee shacabka somaliland ku sugan yihiin , miyaanay siyaasad xumo ahayn inuu safaro maalaa yacniya iska galo hadba dalka iska aado isagoo eegaya danihiisa siyaasadeed.
Ciro ma wuxuu hogaamiye dal ku doonayaa tamashlaynta iyo ku takri falida khasnada golaha wakiilada uu u adeegsacado lacagta qaranku leeyahay hadba siduu doono isagoo uga faaidaysanaya hab qabiil iyo hab shikhsiyadeed intaba, bal qiimee ciro maanta madaxweyne ah dalkana abaartaasi ka jirto siduu wax u maarayn lahaa adigoo hada ka shidaal qaadanaya isku aranta xilalka uu hayo maanta ? runtii waxaa muuqata inaanu waxba maareeyeen oo uu la,aad yahay.
Xisbi nimadu iyadoo ay masuuliyad tahay aad qaranka u hayso maaha in waxkastoo aad yimaada aad xukuumad uun ku eedayso mucaaridnimana maaha inaad xumaha sheegto oo aad buun buuniso waliba been abuur ku dartid iskana indho tirto wanaaga dabcan waxaad mucaaridayso u fiirso kana fiirto waxay keeni karto dhaliisha sheeg lama diidin samaha iyo wanaagana ku dar si aad u noqoto mucaarid fayow oo sama jecel se waa mushkilad inaad noqoto uun xaasid ka xumaada wanaga jecel xumaanta, qaranka mucaarid iyo muxaafidba waa loo siman yahay danta qaranka ee maaha aafooyinka iyo masiibooyinka yimaada inaad xukuumada ku eedayso kursi jaceyl awgigii, kursigana laguma helo afxumo ee wanaag dedaal iyo kalsooni shacab baa lagu yimaadaa.
